L1Menu_CollisionsSmallSystems2025_v1_0_2

This document was generated from an intermediate development snapshot.
  • Comment: Menu for pO, OO, and NeNe 2025 run.

    It uses the 2024 ppRef menu as a baseline. This is to facilitate the comparison between the OO/NeNe and ppRef systems as close as possible.

    The menu for pO, OO, and NeNe presents a suite of L1 seeds for different scenarios for MinimumBias triggering (with and without ZDC, for asymmetric pO or symmetric OO/NeNe collisions).
